\DoxyCodeLine{589 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(AE\_COMPILE\_POLYNOMIALSOLVER) || !defined(AE\_PARTIAL\_BUILD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{590 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{591 \textcolor{comment}{Polynomial root finding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{592 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{593 \textcolor{comment}{This function returns all roots of the polynomial}}
\DoxyCodeLine{594 \textcolor{comment}{    P(x) = a0 + a1*x + a2*x\string^2 + ... + an*x\string^n}}
\DoxyCodeLine{595 \textcolor{comment}{Both real and complex roots are returned (see below).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{596 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{597 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{598 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   array[N+1], polynomial coefficients:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{599 \textcolor{comment}{                * A[0] is constant term}}
\DoxyCodeLine{600 \textcolor{comment}{                * A[N] is a coefficient of X\string^N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{601 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   polynomial degree}}
\DoxyCodeLine{602 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{603 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{604 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array of complex roots:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{605 \textcolor{comment}{                * for isolated real root, X[I] is strictly real: IMAGE(X[I])=0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{606 \textcolor{comment}{                * complex roots are always returned in pairs -\/ roots occupy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{607 \textcolor{comment}{                  positions I and I+1, with:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{608 \textcolor{comment}{                  * X[I+1]=Conj(X[I])}}
\DoxyCodeLine{609 \textcolor{comment}{                  * IMAGE(X[I]) > 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{610 \textcolor{comment}{                  * IMAGE(X[I+1]) = -\/IMAGE(X[I]) < 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{611 \textcolor{comment}{                * multiple real roots may have non-\/zero imaginary part due}}
\DoxyCodeLine{612 \textcolor{comment}{                  to roundoff errors. There is no reliable way to distinguish}}
\DoxyCodeLine{613 \textcolor{comment}{                  real root of multiplicity 2 from two  complex  roots  in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{614 \textcolor{comment}{                  the presence of roundoff errors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{615 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   report, additional information, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{616 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.MaxErr -\/ max( |P(xi)| )  for  i=0..N-\/1.  This  field}}
\DoxyCodeLine{617 \textcolor{comment}{                  allows to quickly estimate "{}quality"{} of the roots  being}}
\DoxyCodeLine{618 \textcolor{comment}{                  returned.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{619 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{620 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:   this function uses companion matrix method to find roots. In  case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{621 \textcolor{comment}{        internal EVD  solver  fails  do  find  eigenvalues,  exception  is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{622 \textcolor{comment}{        generated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{623 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{624 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:   roots are not "{}polished"{} and  no  matrix  balancing  is  performed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{625 \textcolor{comment}{        for them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{626 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{627 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{628 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 24.02.2014 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{629 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{630 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} polynomialsolve(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&a, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1complex__1d__array}{complex\_1d\_array}} \&x, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1polynomialsolverreport}{polynomialsolverreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}

\DoxyCodeLine{632 }
\DoxyCodeLine{633 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(AE\_COMPILE\_DIRECTDENSESOLVERS) || !defined(AE\_PARTIAL\_BUILD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{634 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{635 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver for A*x=b with N*N real matrix A and N*1 real vectorx  x  and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{636 \textcolor{comment}{b. This is "{}slow-\/but-\/feature rich"{} version of the  linear  solver.  Faster}}
\DoxyCodeLine{637 \textcolor{comment}{version is RMatrixSolveFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{638 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{639 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{640 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{641 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{642 \textcolor{comment}{* iterative refinement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{643 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^3) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{644 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{645 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{646 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear  system}}
\DoxyCodeLine{647 \textcolor{comment}{           ! and  performs  iterative   refinement,   which   results   in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{648 \textcolor{comment}{           ! significant performance penalty  when  compared  with  "{}fast"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{649 \textcolor{comment}{           ! version  which  just  performs  LU  decomposition  and  calls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{650 \textcolor{comment}{           ! triangular solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{651 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{652 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This  performance  penalty  is  especially  visible  in   the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{653 \textcolor{comment}{           ! multithreaded mode, because both condition number  estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{654 \textcolor{comment}{           ! and   iterative    refinement   are   inherently   sequential}}
\DoxyCodeLine{655 \textcolor{comment}{           ! calculations. It is also very significant on small matrices.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{656 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{657 \textcolor{comment}{           ! Thus, if you need high performance and if you are pretty sure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{658 \textcolor{comment}{           ! that your system is well conditioned, we  strongly  recommend}}
\DoxyCodeLine{659 \textcolor{comment}{           ! you to use faster solver, RMatrixSolveFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{660 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{661 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{662 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], system matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{663 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{664 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{665 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{666 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{667 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{668 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    matrix is very badly conditioned or exactly singular.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{669 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{670 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved (but matrix A may be ill-\/conditioned,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{671 \textcolor{comment}{                        check R1/RInf parameters for condition numbers).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{672 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   additional report, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{673 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.r1    condition number in 1-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{674 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.rinf  condition number in inf-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{675 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], it contains:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{676 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{677 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{678 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{679 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{680 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{681 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Free Edition of ALGLIB supports following important features for  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{682 \textcolor{comment}{  ! function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{683 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C++ version: x64 SIMD support using C++ intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{684 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C\#  version: x64 SIMD support using NET5/NetCore hardware intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{685 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{686 \textcolor{comment}{  ! We  recommend  you  to  read  'Compiling ALGLIB' section of the ALGLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{687 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Reference Manual in order  to  find  out  how to activate SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{688 \textcolor{comment}{  ! in ALGLIB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{689 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{690 \textcolor{comment}{  ! COMMERCIAL EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{691 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{692 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Commercial Edition of ALGLIB includes following important improvements}}
\DoxyCodeLine{693 \textcolor{comment}{  ! of this function:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{706 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} rmatrixsolve(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__2d__array}{real\_2d\_array}} \&a, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&b, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1densesolverreport}{densesolverreport}} \&rep, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}

\DoxyCodeLine{709 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{710 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{711 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{712 \textcolor{comment}{This  subroutine  solves  a  system  A*x=b,  where A is NxN non-\/denegerate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{713 \textcolor{comment}{real matrix, x  and  b  are  vectors.  This is a "{}fast"{} version of  linear}}
\DoxyCodeLine{714 \textcolor{comment}{solver which does NOT provide  any  additional  functions  like  condition}}
\DoxyCodeLine{715 \textcolor{comment}{number estimation or iterative refinement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{716 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{717 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{718 \textcolor{comment}{* efficient algorithm O(N\string^3) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{719 \textcolor{comment}{* no performance overhead from additional functionality}}
\DoxyCodeLine{720 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{721 \textcolor{comment}{If you need condition number estimation or iterative refinement, use  more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{722 \textcolor{comment}{feature-\/rich version -\/ RMatrixSolve().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{723 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{724 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{725 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], system matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{726 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{727 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{728 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{729 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{730 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{731 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    matrix is exactly singular (ill conditioned matrices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{732 \textcolor{comment}{                        are not recognized).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{733 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{734 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{735 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[N]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{736 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  overwritten by solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{737 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}

\DoxyCodeLine{769 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{770 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{771 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{772 \textcolor{comment}{Similar to RMatrixSolve() but solves task with multiple right parts (where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{773 \textcolor{comment}{b and x are NxM matrices). This is  "{}slow-\/but-\/robust"{}  version  of  linear}}
\DoxyCodeLine{774 \textcolor{comment}{solver with additional functionality  like  condition  number  estimation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{775 \textcolor{comment}{There also exists faster version -\/ RMatrixSolveMFast().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{776 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{777 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{778 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{779 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{780 \textcolor{comment}{* optional iterative refinement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{781 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^3+M*N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{782 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{783 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{784 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear  system}}
\DoxyCodeLine{785 \textcolor{comment}{           ! and  performs  iterative   refinement,   which   results   in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{786 \textcolor{comment}{           ! significant performance penalty  when  compared  with  "{}fast"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{787 \textcolor{comment}{           ! version  which  just  performs  LU  decomposition  and  calls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{788 \textcolor{comment}{           ! triangular solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{789 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{790 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This  performance  penalty  is  especially  visible  in   the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{791 \textcolor{comment}{           ! multithreaded mode, because both condition number  estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{792 \textcolor{comment}{           ! and   iterative    refinement   are   inherently   sequential}}
\DoxyCodeLine{793 \textcolor{comment}{           ! calculations. It also very significant on small matrices.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{794 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{795 \textcolor{comment}{           ! Thus, if you need high performance and if you are pretty sure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{796 \textcolor{comment}{           ! that your system is well conditioned, we  strongly  recommend}}
\DoxyCodeLine{797 \textcolor{comment}{           ! you to use faster solver, RMatrixSolveMFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{798 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{799 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{800 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], system matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{801 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{802 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..M-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{803 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   right part size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{804 \textcolor{comment}{    RFS     -\/   iterative refinement switch:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{805 \textcolor{comment}{                * True -\/ refinement is used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{806 \textcolor{comment}{                  Less performance, more precision.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{807 \textcolor{comment}{                * False -\/ refinement is not used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{808 \textcolor{comment}{                  More performance, less precision.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{809 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{810 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{811 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{812 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    A is ill conditioned or singular.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{813 \textcolor{comment}{                        X is filled by zeros in such cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{814 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{815 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved (but matrix A may be ill-\/conditioned,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{816 \textcolor{comment}{                        check R1/RInf parameters for condition numbers).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{817 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   additional report, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{818 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.r1    condition number in 1-\/norm}}

\DoxyCodeLine{821 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{822 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}

\DoxyCodeLine{854 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{855 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{856 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{857 \textcolor{comment}{Similar to RMatrixSolve() but solves task with multiple right parts (where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{858 \textcolor{comment}{b and x are NxM matrices). This is "{}fast"{} version of linear  solver  which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{859 \textcolor{comment}{does NOT offer additional functions like condition  number  estimation  or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{860 \textcolor{comment}{iterative refinement.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{863 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^3+M*N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{864 \textcolor{comment}{* no additional functionality, highest performance}}

\DoxyCodeLine{919 }
\DoxyCodeLine{920 }
\DoxyCodeLine{921 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{922 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{923 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{924 \textcolor{comment}{This  subroutine  solves  a  system  A*x=b,  where A is NxN non-\/denegerate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{925 \textcolor{comment}{real matrix given by its LU decomposition, x and b are real vectors.  This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{926 \textcolor{comment}{is "{}slow-\/but-\/robust"{} version of the linear LU-\/based solver. Faster version}}
\DoxyCodeLine{927 \textcolor{comment}{is RMatrixLUSolveFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{928 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{929 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{930 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{931 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{932 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{933 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{934 \textcolor{comment}{No iterative refinement  is provided because exact form of original matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{935 \textcolor{comment}{is not known to subroutine. Use RMatrixSolve or RMatrixMixedSolve  if  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{936 \textcolor{comment}{need iterative refinement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{937 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{938 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{939 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear system,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{940 \textcolor{comment}{           ! which results in 10-\/15x  performance  penalty  when  compared}}
\DoxyCodeLine{941 \textcolor{comment}{           ! with "{}fast"{} version which just calls triangular solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{942 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{943 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This performance penalty is insignificant  when compared with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{944 \textcolor{comment}{           ! cost of large LU decomposition.  However,  if you  call  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{945 \textcolor{comment}{           ! function many times for the same  left  side,  this  overhead}}
\DoxyCodeLine{946 \textcolor{comment}{           ! BECOMES significant. It  also  becomes significant for small-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{947 \textcolor{comment}{           ! scale problems.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{948 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{949 \textcolor{comment}{           ! In such cases we strongly recommend you to use faster solver,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{950 \textcolor{comment}{           ! RMatrixLUSolveFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{951 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{952 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{953 \textcolor{comment}{    LUA     -\/   array[N,N], LU decomposition, RMatrixLU result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{954 \textcolor{comment}{    P       -\/   array[N], pivots array, RMatrixLU result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{955 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{956 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[N], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{957 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{958 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{959 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{960 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    matrix is very badly conditioned or exactly singular.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{961 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{962 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved (but matrix A may be ill-\/conditioned,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{963 \textcolor{comment}{                        check R1/RInf parameters for condition numbers).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{964 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   additional report, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{965 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.r1    condition number in 1-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{966 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.rinf  condition number in inf-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{967 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], it contains:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{968 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{969 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{970 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{971 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{972 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{973 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 27.01.2010 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{974 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{975 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} rmatrixlusolve(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__2d__array}{real\_2d\_array}} \&lua, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1integer__1d__array}{integer\_1d\_array}} \&p, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&b, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1densesolverreport}{densesolverreport}} \&rep, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}

\DoxyCodeLine{1013 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1014 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1015 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1016 \textcolor{comment}{Similar to RMatrixLUSolve() but solves  task  with  multiple  right  parts}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1017 \textcolor{comment}{(where b and x are NxM matrices). This  is  "{}robust-\/but-\/slow"{}  version  of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1018 \textcolor{comment}{LU-\/based solver which performs additional  checks  for  non-\/degeneracy  of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1019 \textcolor{comment}{inputs (condition number estimation). If you need  best  performance,  use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1020 \textcolor{comment}{"{}fast-\/without-\/any-\/checks"{} version, RMatrixLUSolveMFast().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1021 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1022 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1023 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1024 \textcolor{comment}{* O(M*N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1025 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1026 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1027 \textcolor{comment}{No iterative refinement  is provided because exact form of original matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1028 \textcolor{comment}{is not known to subroutine. Use RMatrixSolve or RMatrixMixedSolve  if  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1029 \textcolor{comment}{need iterative refinement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1030 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1031 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1032 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear system,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1033 \textcolor{comment}{           ! which  results  in  significant  performance   penalty   when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1034 \textcolor{comment}{           ! compared with "{}fast"{}  version  which  just  calls  triangular}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1035 \textcolor{comment}{           ! solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1036 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1037 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This performance penalty is especially apparent when you  use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1038 \textcolor{comment}{           ! ALGLIB parallel capabilities (condition number estimation  is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1039 \textcolor{comment}{           ! inherently  sequential).  It   also   becomes significant for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1040 \textcolor{comment}{           ! small-\/scale problems.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1041 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1042 \textcolor{comment}{           ! In such cases we strongly recommend you to use faster solver,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1043 \textcolor{comment}{           ! RMatrixLUSolveMFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1044 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1045 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1046 \textcolor{comment}{    LUA     -\/   array[N,N], LU decomposition, RMatrixLU result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1047 \textcolor{comment}{    P       -\/   array[N], pivots array, RMatrixLU result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1048 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1049 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..M-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1050 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   right part size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1051 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1052 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1053 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1054 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    matrix is very badly conditioned or exactly singular.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1055 \textcolor{comment}{                        X is filled by zeros in such cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1056 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1057 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved (but matrix A may be ill-\/conditioned,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1058 \textcolor{comment}{                        check R1/RInf parameters for condition numbers).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1059 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   additional report, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1060 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.r1    condition number in 1-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1061 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.rinf  condition number in inf-\/norm}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1063 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1064 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1094 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1095 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1096 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1097 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1098 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1099 \textcolor{comment}{Similar to RMatrixLUSolve() but solves  task  with  multiple  right parts,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1100 \textcolor{comment}{where b and x are NxM matrices.  This is "{}fast-\/without-\/any-\/checks"{} version}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1101 \textcolor{comment}{of LU-\/based solver. It does not estimate  condition number  of  a  system,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1102 \textcolor{comment}{so it is extremely fast. If you need better detection  of  near-\/degenerate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1103 \textcolor{comment}{cases, use RMatrixLUSolveM() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1104 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1105 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1106 \textcolor{comment}{* O(M*N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1107 \textcolor{comment}{* fast algorithm without ANY additional checks, just triangular solver}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1108 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1109 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1110 \textcolor{comment}{    LUA     -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], LU decomposition, RMatrixLU result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1111 \textcolor{comment}{    P       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], pivots array, RMatrixLU result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1112 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1113 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..M-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1114 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   right part size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1115 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1116 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1117 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1118 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    matrix is exactly singular (ill conditioned matrices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1119 \textcolor{comment}{                        are not recognized).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1120 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1121 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1122 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[N,M]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1123 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  overwritten by solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1124 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1125 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1126 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1127 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1131 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C\#  version: x64 SIMD support using NET5/NetCore hardware intrinsics}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1156 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1157 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1158 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1159 \textcolor{comment}{This  subroutine  solves  a  system  A*x=b,  where BOTH ORIGINAL A AND ITS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1160 \textcolor{comment}{LU DECOMPOSITION ARE KNOWN. You can use it if for some  reasons  you  have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1161 \textcolor{comment}{both A and its LU decomposition.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1162 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1163 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1164 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1165 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1166 \textcolor{comment}{* iterative refinement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1167 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1168 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1169 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1170 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], system matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1171 \textcolor{comment}{    LUA     -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], LU decomposition, RMatrixLU result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1172 \textcolor{comment}{    P       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], pivots array, RMatrixLU result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1173 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1174 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1175 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1176 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1177 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1178 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    matrix is very badly conditioned or exactly singular.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1179 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1180 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved (but matrix A may be ill-\/conditioned,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1181 \textcolor{comment}{                        check R1/RInf parameters for condition numbers).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1182 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   additional report, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1183 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.r1    condition number in 1-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1184 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.rinf  condition number in inf-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1185 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], it contains:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1186 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1187 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1188 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1189 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1234 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1235 \textcolor{comment}{Complex dense solver for A*X=B with N*N  complex  matrix  A,  N*M  complex}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1236 \textcolor{comment}{matrices  X  and  B.  "{}Slow-\/but-\/feature-\/rich"{}   version   which   provides}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1237 \textcolor{comment}{additional functions, at the cost of slower  performance.  Faster  version}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1238 \textcolor{comment}{may be invoked with CMatrixSolveMFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1239 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1240 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1241 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1242 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1243 \textcolor{comment}{* iterative refinement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1244 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^3+M*N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1245 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1246 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1247 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear  system}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1248 \textcolor{comment}{           ! and  performs  iterative   refinement,   which   results   in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1249 \textcolor{comment}{           ! significant performance penalty  when  compared  with  "{}fast"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1250 \textcolor{comment}{           ! version  which  just  performs  LU  decomposition  and  calls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1251 \textcolor{comment}{           ! triangular solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1252 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1253 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This  performance  penalty  is  especially  visible  in   the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1254 \textcolor{comment}{           ! multithreaded mode, because both condition number  estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1255 \textcolor{comment}{           ! and   iterative    refinement   are   inherently   sequential}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1256 \textcolor{comment}{           ! calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1257 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1258 \textcolor{comment}{           ! Thus, if you need high performance and if you are pretty sure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1259 \textcolor{comment}{           ! that your system is well conditioned, we  strongly  recommend}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1260 \textcolor{comment}{           ! you to use faster solver, CMatrixSolveMFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1261 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1262 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1263 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], system matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1264 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1265 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..M-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1266 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   right part size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1267 \textcolor{comment}{    RFS     -\/   iterative refinement switch:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1268 \textcolor{comment}{                * True -\/ refinement is used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1269 \textcolor{comment}{                  Less performance, more precision.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1270 \textcolor{comment}{                * False -\/ refinement is not used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1271 \textcolor{comment}{                  More performance, less precision.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1272 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1273 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1274 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1275 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    matrix is very badly conditioned or exactly singular.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1276 \textcolor{comment}{                        X is filled by zeros in such cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1277 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1278 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved (but matrix A may be ill-\/conditioned,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1279 \textcolor{comment}{                        check R1/RInf parameters for condition numbers).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1280 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   additional report, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1281 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.r1    condition number in 1-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1282 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.rinf  condition number in inf-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1283 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N,M], it contains:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1284 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1285 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1286 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1287 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1288 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1289 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Free Edition of ALGLIB supports following important features for  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1290 \textcolor{comment}{  ! function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1291 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C++ version: x64 SIMD support using C++ intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1292 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C\#  version: x64 SIMD support using NET5/NetCore hardware intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1293 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1294 \textcolor{comment}{  ! We  recommend  you  to  read  'Compiling ALGLIB' section of the ALGLIB}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1317 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1318 \textcolor{comment}{Complex dense solver for A*X=B with N*N  complex  matrix  A,  N*M  complex}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1319 \textcolor{comment}{matrices  X  and  B.  "{}Fast-\/but-\/lightweight"{} version which  provides  just}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1373 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1374 \textcolor{comment}{Complex dense solver for A*x=B with N*N complex matrix A and  N*1  complex}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1375 \textcolor{comment}{vectors x and b. "{}Slow-\/but-\/feature-\/rich"{} version of the solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1376 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1377 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1378 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1379 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1380 \textcolor{comment}{* iterative refinement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1381 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^3) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1382 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1383 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1384 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear  system}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1385 \textcolor{comment}{           ! and  performs  iterative   refinement,   which   results   in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1386 \textcolor{comment}{           ! significant performance penalty  when  compared  with  "{}fast"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1387 \textcolor{comment}{           ! version  which  just  performs  LU  decomposition  and  calls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1388 \textcolor{comment}{           ! triangular solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1389 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1390 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This  performance  penalty  is  especially  visible  in   the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1391 \textcolor{comment}{           ! multithreaded mode, because both condition number  estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1392 \textcolor{comment}{           ! and   iterative    refinement   are   inherently   sequential}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1393 \textcolor{comment}{           ! calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1394 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1395 \textcolor{comment}{           ! Thus, if you need high performance and if you are pretty sure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1396 \textcolor{comment}{           ! that your system is well conditioned, we  strongly  recommend}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1397 \textcolor{comment}{           ! you to use faster solver, CMatrixSolveFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1398 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1399 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1400 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], system matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1401 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1402 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1403 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1404 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1405 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1406 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    matrix is very badly conditioned or exactly singular.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1407 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1408 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved (but matrix A may be ill-\/conditioned,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1409 \textcolor{comment}{                        check R1/RInf parameters for condition numbers).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1410 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   additional report, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1411 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.r1    condition number in 1-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1412 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.rinf  condition number in inf-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1413 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], it contains:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1414 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1415 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1416 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1417 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1418 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1419 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Free Edition of ALGLIB supports following important features for  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1420 \textcolor{comment}{  ! function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1421 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C++ version: x64 SIMD support using C++ intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1422 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C\#  version: x64 SIMD support using NET5/NetCore hardware intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1423 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1424 \textcolor{comment}{  ! We  recommend  you  to  read  'Compiling ALGLIB' section of the ALGLIB}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1500 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1501 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver for A*X=B with N*N complex A given by its  LU  decomposition,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1502 \textcolor{comment}{and N*M matrices X and B (multiple right sides).   "{}Slow-\/but-\/feature-\/rich"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1503 \textcolor{comment}{version of the solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1504 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1505 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1506 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1507 \textcolor{comment}{* O(M*N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1508 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1509 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1510 \textcolor{comment}{No iterative refinement  is provided because exact form of original matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1511 \textcolor{comment}{is not known to subroutine. Use CMatrixSolve or CMatrixMixedSolve  if  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1512 \textcolor{comment}{need iterative refinement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1513 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1514 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1515 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear system,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1516 \textcolor{comment}{           ! which  results  in  significant  performance   penalty   when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1517 \textcolor{comment}{           ! compared with "{}fast"{}  version  which  just  calls  triangular}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1518 \textcolor{comment}{           ! solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1519 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1520 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This performance penalty is especially apparent when you  use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1521 \textcolor{comment}{           ! ALGLIB parallel capabilities (condition number estimation  is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1522 \textcolor{comment}{           ! inherently  sequential).  It   also   becomes significant for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1523 \textcolor{comment}{           ! small-\/scale problems.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1524 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1525 \textcolor{comment}{           ! In such cases we strongly recommend you to use faster solver,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1526 \textcolor{comment}{           ! CMatrixLUSolveMFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1527 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1528 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1529 \textcolor{comment}{    LUA     -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], LU decomposition, RMatrixLU result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1530 \textcolor{comment}{    P       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], pivots array, RMatrixLU result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1531 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1539 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved (but matrix A may be ill-\/conditioned,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1598 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1599 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1600 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[N,M]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1601 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  overwritten by solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1602 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1633 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1634 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1635 \textcolor{comment}{Complex dense linear solver for A*x=b with complex N*N A  given  by its LU}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1636 \textcolor{comment}{decomposition and N*1 vectors x and b. This is  "{}slow-\/but-\/robust"{}  version}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1637 \textcolor{comment}{of  the  complex  linear  solver  with  additional  features   which   add}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1638 \textcolor{comment}{significant performance overhead. Faster version  is  CMatrixLUSolveFast()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1639 \textcolor{comment}{function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1640 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1641 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1642 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1643 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1644 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1645 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1646 \textcolor{comment}{No iterative refinement is provided because exact form of original matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1647 \textcolor{comment}{is not known to subroutine. Use CMatrixSolve or CMatrixMixedSolve  if  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1648 \textcolor{comment}{need iterative refinement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1649 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1650 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1651 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear system,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1652 \textcolor{comment}{           ! which results in 10-\/15x  performance  penalty  when  compared}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1653 \textcolor{comment}{           ! with "{}fast"{} version which just calls triangular solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1654 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1655 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This performance penalty is insignificant  when compared with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1656 \textcolor{comment}{           ! cost of large LU decomposition.  However,  if you  call  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1657 \textcolor{comment}{           ! function many times for the same  left  side,  this  overhead}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1658 \textcolor{comment}{           ! BECOMES significant. It  also  becomes significant for small-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1659 \textcolor{comment}{           ! scale problems.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1660 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1661 \textcolor{comment}{           ! In such cases we strongly recommend you to use faster solver,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1662 \textcolor{comment}{           ! CMatrixLUSolveFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1663 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1664 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1665 \textcolor{comment}{    LUA     -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], LU decomposition, CMatrixLU result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1666 \textcolor{comment}{    P       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], pivots array, CMatrixLU result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1667 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1668 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1669 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1670 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1671 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1672 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    matrix is very badly conditioned or exactly singular.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1673 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1674 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved (but matrix A may be ill-\/conditioned,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1675 \textcolor{comment}{                        check R1/RInf parameters for condition numbers).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1676 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   additional report, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1677 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.r1    condition number in 1-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1678 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.rinf  condition number in inf-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1679 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], it contains:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1680 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1681 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1682 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1683 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1684 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 27.01.2010 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1685 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1797 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1798 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1799 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver for A*X=B with N*N symmetric positive definite matrix A,  and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1800 \textcolor{comment}{N*M vectors X and B. It is "{}slow-\/but-\/feature-\/rich"{} version of the solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1801 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1802 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1803 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1804 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1805 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^3+M*N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1806 \textcolor{comment}{* matrix is represented by its upper or lower triangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1807 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1808 \textcolor{comment}{No iterative refinement is provided because such partial representation of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1809 \textcolor{comment}{matrix does not allow efficient calculation of extra-\/precise  matrix-\/vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1810 \textcolor{comment}{products for large matrices. Use RMatrixSolve or RMatrixMixedSolve  if  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1811 \textcolor{comment}{need iterative refinement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1812 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1813 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1814 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear system,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1815 \textcolor{comment}{           ! which  results  in  significant   performance   penalty  when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1816 \textcolor{comment}{           ! compared with "{}fast"{} version  which  just  performs  Cholesky}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1817 \textcolor{comment}{           ! decomposition and calls triangular solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1818 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1819 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This  performance  penalty  is  especially  visible  in   the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1820 \textcolor{comment}{           ! multithreaded mode, because both condition number  estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1821 \textcolor{comment}{           ! and   iterative    refinement   are   inherently   sequential}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1822 \textcolor{comment}{           ! calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1823 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1824 \textcolor{comment}{           ! Thus, if you need high performance and if you are pretty sure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1825 \textcolor{comment}{           ! that your system is well conditioned, we  strongly  recommend}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1826 \textcolor{comment}{           ! you to use faster solver, SPDMatrixSolveMFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1827 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1828 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1829 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], system matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1830 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1831 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   what half of A is provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1832 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..M-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1833 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   right part size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1834 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1835 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1836 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1837 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    matrix is very badly conditioned or non-\/SPD.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1838 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1839 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved (but matrix A may be ill-\/conditioned,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1840 \textcolor{comment}{                        check R1/RInf parameters for condition numbers).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1841 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   additional report, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1842 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.r1    condition number in 1-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1843 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.rinf  condition number in inf-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1844 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N,M], it contains:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1845 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1846 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1847 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1848 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1849 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1850 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Free Edition of ALGLIB supports following important features for  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1851 \textcolor{comment}{  ! function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1852 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C++ version: x64 SIMD support using C++ intrinsics}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1878 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1879 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver for A*X=B with N*N symmetric positive definite matrix A,  and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1880 \textcolor{comment}{N*M vectors X and B. It is "{}fast-\/but-\/lightweight"{} version of the solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1881 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1882 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1883 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^3+M*N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1884 \textcolor{comment}{* matrix is represented by its upper or lower triangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1885 \textcolor{comment}{* no additional time consuming features}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1886 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1887 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1888 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], system matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1889 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1890 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   what half of A is provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1891 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..M-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1892 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   right part size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1893 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1894 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1895 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1896 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    A is is exactly singular}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1897 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1898 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task was solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1899 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[N,M], it contains:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1900 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1901 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1902 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1932 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1933 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1934 \textcolor{comment}{Dense linear solver for A*x=b with N*N real  symmetric  positive  definite}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1935 \textcolor{comment}{matrix A,  N*1 vectors x and b.  "{}Slow-\/but-\/feature-\/rich"{}  version  of  the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1936 \textcolor{comment}{solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1937 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1938 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1939 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1940 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1941 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^3) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1942 \textcolor{comment}{* matrix is represented by its upper or lower triangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1943 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1944 \textcolor{comment}{No iterative refinement is provided because such partial representation of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1945 \textcolor{comment}{matrix does not allow efficient calculation of extra-\/precise  matrix-\/vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1946 \textcolor{comment}{products for large matrices. Use RMatrixSolve or RMatrixMixedSolve  if  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1947 \textcolor{comment}{need iterative refinement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1948 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1949 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1950 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear system,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1951 \textcolor{comment}{           ! which  results  in  significant   performance   penalty  when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1952 \textcolor{comment}{           ! compared with "{}fast"{} version  which  just  performs  Cholesky}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1953 \textcolor{comment}{           ! decomposition and calls triangular solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1954 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1955 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This  performance  penalty  is  especially  visible  in   the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1956 \textcolor{comment}{           ! multithreaded mode, because both condition number  estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1957 \textcolor{comment}{           ! and   iterative    refinement   are   inherently   sequential}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1958 \textcolor{comment}{           ! calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1959 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1960 \textcolor{comment}{           ! Thus, if you need high performance and if you are pretty sure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1961 \textcolor{comment}{           ! that your system is well conditioned, we  strongly  recommend}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1962 \textcolor{comment}{           ! you to use faster solver, SPDMatrixSolveFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1963 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1964 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1965 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], system matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1966 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1967 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   what half of A is provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1968 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1969 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1970 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1971 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1972 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    matrix is very badly conditioned or non-\/SPD.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1973 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1974 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved (but matrix A may be ill-\/conditioned,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1975 \textcolor{comment}{                        check R1/RInf parameters for condition numbers).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1976 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   additional report, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1977 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.r1    condition number in 1-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1978 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.rinf  condition number in inf-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1979 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], it contains:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1980 \textcolor{comment}{                * info>0    =>  solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1981 \textcolor{comment}{                * info=-\/3   =>  filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1982 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1983 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1984 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1985 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Free Edition of ALGLIB supports following important features for  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1986 \textcolor{comment}{  ! function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1987 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C++ version: x64 SIMD support using C++ intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1988 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C\#  version: x64 SIMD support using NET5/NetCore hardware intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1989 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1990 \textcolor{comment}{  ! We  recommend  you  to  read  'Compiling ALGLIB' section of the ALGLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1991 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Reference Manual in order  to  find  out  how to activate SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1992 \textcolor{comment}{  ! in ALGLIB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1993 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2067 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2068 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2069 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver for A*X=B with N*N symmetric positive definite matrix A given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2070 \textcolor{comment}{by its Cholesky decomposition, and N*M vectors X and B. It  is  "{}slow-\/but-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2071 \textcolor{comment}{feature-\/rich"{} version of the solver which estimates  condition  number  of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2072 \textcolor{comment}{the system.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2073 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2074 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2075 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2076 \textcolor{comment}{* O(M*N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2077 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2078 \textcolor{comment}{* matrix is represented by its upper or lower triangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2079 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2080 \textcolor{comment}{No iterative refinement is provided because such partial representation of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2081 \textcolor{comment}{matrix does not allow efficient calculation of extra-\/precise  matrix-\/vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2082 \textcolor{comment}{products for large matrices. Use RMatrixSolve or RMatrixMixedSolve  if  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2083 \textcolor{comment}{need iterative refinement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2084 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2085 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2086 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear system,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2087 \textcolor{comment}{           ! which  results  in  significant  performance   penalty   when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2088 \textcolor{comment}{           ! compared with "{}fast"{}  version  which  just  calls  triangular}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2089 \textcolor{comment}{           ! solver. Amount of  overhead  introduced  depends  on  M  (the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2090 \textcolor{comment}{           ! larger -\/ the more efficient).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2091 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2092 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This performance penalty is insignificant  when compared with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2093 \textcolor{comment}{           ! cost of large LU decomposition.  However,  if you  call  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2094 \textcolor{comment}{           ! function many times for the same  left  side,  this  overhead}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2095 \textcolor{comment}{           ! BECOMES significant. It  also  becomes significant for small-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2096 \textcolor{comment}{           ! scale problems (N<50).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2097 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2098 \textcolor{comment}{           ! In such cases we strongly recommend you to use faster solver,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2099 \textcolor{comment}{           ! SPDMatrixCholeskySolveMFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2100 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2101 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2102 \textcolor{comment}{    CHA     -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], Cholesky decomposition,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2103 \textcolor{comment}{                SPDMatrixCholesky result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2104 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of CHA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2105 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   what half of CHA is provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2106 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..M-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2107 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   right part size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2108 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2109 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2110 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2111 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    A is is exactly singular or badly conditioned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2112 \textcolor{comment}{                        X is filled by zeros in such cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2113 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2114 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task was solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2115 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   additional report, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2116 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.r1    condition number in 1-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2117 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.rinf  condition number in inf-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2118 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2119 \textcolor{comment}{                * for info>0 contains solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2120 \textcolor{comment}{                * for info=-\/3 filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2121 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2122 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2128 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2129 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver for A*X=B with N*N symmetric positive definite matrix A given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2130 \textcolor{comment}{by its Cholesky decomposition, and N*M vectors X and B. It  is  "{}fast-\/but-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2131 \textcolor{comment}{lightweight"{} version of  the  solver  which  just  solves  linear  system,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2132 \textcolor{comment}{without any additional functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2133 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2134 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2135 \textcolor{comment}{* O(M*N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2136 \textcolor{comment}{* matrix is represented by its upper or lower triangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2137 \textcolor{comment}{* no additional functionality}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2138 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2139 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2140 \textcolor{comment}{    CHA     -\/   array[N,N], Cholesky decomposition,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2141 \textcolor{comment}{                SPDMatrixCholesky result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2142 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of CHA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2143 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   what half of CHA is provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2144 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[N,M], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2145 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   right part size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2146 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2147 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2148 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2149 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    A is is exactly singular or badly conditioned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2150 \textcolor{comment}{                        X is filled by zeros in such cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2151 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2152 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task was solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2153 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[N]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2154 \textcolor{comment}{                * for info>0 overwritten by solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2155 \textcolor{comment}{                * for info=-\/3 filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2156 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2157 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2158 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 18.03.2015 by Bochkanov Sergey}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2161 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2162 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2163 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2164 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver for A*x=b with N*N symmetric positive definite matrix A given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2165 \textcolor{comment}{by its Cholesky decomposition, and N*1 real vectors x and b. This is "{}slow-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2166 \textcolor{comment}{but-\/feature-\/rich"{}  version  of  the  solver  which,  in  addition  to  the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2167 \textcolor{comment}{solution, performs condition number estimation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2168 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2169 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2170 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2171 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2172 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2173 \textcolor{comment}{* matrix is represented by its upper or lower triangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2174 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2175 \textcolor{comment}{No iterative refinement is provided because such partial representation of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2176 \textcolor{comment}{matrix does not allow efficient calculation of extra-\/precise  matrix-\/vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2177 \textcolor{comment}{products for large matrices. Use RMatrixSolve or RMatrixMixedSolve  if  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2178 \textcolor{comment}{need iterative refinement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2179 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2180 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2181 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear system,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2182 \textcolor{comment}{           ! which results in 10-\/15x  performance  penalty  when  compared}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2183 \textcolor{comment}{           ! with "{}fast"{} version which just calls triangular solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2184 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2185 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This performance penalty is insignificant  when compared with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2186 \textcolor{comment}{           ! cost of large LU decomposition.  However,  if you  call  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2187 \textcolor{comment}{           ! function many times for the same  left  side,  this  overhead}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2188 \textcolor{comment}{           ! BECOMES significant. It  also  becomes significant for small-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2189 \textcolor{comment}{           ! scale problems (N<50).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2190 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2191 \textcolor{comment}{           ! In such cases we strongly recommend you to use faster solver,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2192 \textcolor{comment}{           ! SPDMatrixCholeskySolveFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2193 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2194 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2195 \textcolor{comment}{    CHA     -\/   array[N,N], Cholesky decomposition,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2196 \textcolor{comment}{                SPDMatrixCholesky result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2197 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2198 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   what half of CHA is provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2199 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[N], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2200 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2201 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2202 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2203 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    A is is exactly singular or ill conditioned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2204 \textcolor{comment}{                        X is filled by zeros in such cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2205 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2206 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2207 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   additional report, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2208 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.r1    condition number in 1-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2209 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.rinf  condition number in inf-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2210 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2211 \textcolor{comment}{                * for info>0  -\/ solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2212 \textcolor{comment}{                * for info=-\/3 -\/ filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2213 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2214 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2215 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 27.01.2010 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2216 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
