\DoxyCodeLine{2382 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2383 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver for A*x=b, with N*N Hermitian positive definite matrix A, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2384 \textcolor{comment}{N*1 complex vectors  x  and  b.  "{}Slow-\/but-\/feature-\/rich"{}  version  of  the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2385 \textcolor{comment}{solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2386 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2387 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2388 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2389 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2390 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^3) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2391 \textcolor{comment}{* matrix is represented by its upper or lower triangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2392 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2393 \textcolor{comment}{No iterative refinement is provided because such partial representation of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2394 \textcolor{comment}{matrix does not allow efficient calculation of extra-\/precise  matrix-\/vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2395 \textcolor{comment}{products for large matrices. Use RMatrixSolve or RMatrixMixedSolve  if  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2396 \textcolor{comment}{need iterative refinement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2397 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2398 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2399 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear system,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2400 \textcolor{comment}{           ! which  results  in  significant   performance   penalty  when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2401 \textcolor{comment}{           ! compared with "{}fast"{} version  which  just  performs  Cholesky}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2402 \textcolor{comment}{           ! decomposition and calls triangular solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2403 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2404 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This  performance  penalty  is  especially  visible  in   the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2405 \textcolor{comment}{           ! multithreaded mode, because both condition number  estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2406 \textcolor{comment}{           ! and   iterative    refinement   are   inherently   sequential}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2407 \textcolor{comment}{           ! calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2408 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2409 \textcolor{comment}{           ! Thus, if you need high performance and if you are pretty sure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2410 \textcolor{comment}{           ! that your system is well conditioned, we  strongly  recommend}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2411 \textcolor{comment}{           ! you to use faster solver, HPDMatrixSolveFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2412 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2413 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2414 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], system matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2415 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2416 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   what half of A is provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2417 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2418 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2419 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2420 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   same as in RMatrixSolve}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2421 \textcolor{comment}{                Returns -\/3 for non-\/HPD matrices.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2422 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   same as in RMatrixSolve}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2423 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   same as in RMatrixSolve}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2424 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2425 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2426 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2427 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Free Edition of ALGLIB supports following important features for  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2428 \textcolor{comment}{  ! function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2429 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C++ version: x64 SIMD support using C++ intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2430 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C\#  version: x64 SIMD support using NET5/NetCore hardware intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2431 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2432 \textcolor{comment}{  ! We  recommend  you  to  read  'Compiling ALGLIB' section of the ALGLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2433 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Reference Manual in order  to  find  out  how to activate SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2434 \textcolor{comment}{  ! in ALGLIB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2435 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2436 \textcolor{comment}{  ! COMMERCIAL EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2437 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2438 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Commercial Edition of ALGLIB includes following important improvements}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2439 \textcolor{comment}{  ! of this function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2440 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * high-\/performance native backend with same C\# interface (C\# version)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2441 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * multithreading support (C++ and C\# versions)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2442 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * hardware vendor (Intel) implementations of linear algebra primitives}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2443 \textcolor{comment}{  !   (C++ and C\# versions, x86/x64 platform)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2452 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} hpdmatrixsolve(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1complex__2d__array}{complex\_2d\_array}} \&a, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} isupper, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1complex__1d__array}{complex\_1d\_array}} \&b, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1densesolverreport}{densesolverreport}} \&rep, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1complex__1d__array}{complex\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}

\DoxyCodeLine{2454 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2455 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2456 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver for A*x=b, with N*N Hermitian positive definite matrix A, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2457 \textcolor{comment}{N*1 complex vectors  x  and  b.  "{}Fast-\/but-\/lightweight"{}  version  of   the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2458 \textcolor{comment}{solver without additional functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2459 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2460 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2461 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^3) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2462 \textcolor{comment}{* matrix is represented by its upper or lower triangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2463 \textcolor{comment}{* no additional time consuming functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2464 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2465 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2466 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], system matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2467 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2468 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   what half of A is provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2469 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2470 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2471 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2472 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2473 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    A is is exactly singular or not positive definite}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2474 \textcolor{comment}{                        X is filled by zeros in such cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2475 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2476 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task was solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2477 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2478 \textcolor{comment}{                * overwritten by solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2479 \textcolor{comment}{                * zeros, if A is exactly singular (diagonal of its LU}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2480 \textcolor{comment}{                  decomposition has exact zeros).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2481 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2482 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2488 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2510 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2511 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2512 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2513 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver for A*X=B with N*N Hermitian positive definite matrix A given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2514 \textcolor{comment}{by its Cholesky decomposition and N*M complex matrices X  and  B.  This is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2515 \textcolor{comment}{"{}slow-\/but-\/feature-\/rich"{} version of the solver which, in  addition  to  the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2516 \textcolor{comment}{solution, estimates condition number of the system.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2517 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2518 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2519 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2520 \textcolor{comment}{* O(M*N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2521 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2522 \textcolor{comment}{* matrix is represented by its upper or lower triangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2523 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2524 \textcolor{comment}{No iterative refinement is provided because such partial representation of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2525 \textcolor{comment}{matrix does not allow efficient calculation of extra-\/precise  matrix-\/vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2526 \textcolor{comment}{products for large matrices. Use RMatrixSolve or RMatrixMixedSolve  if  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2527 \textcolor{comment}{need iterative refinement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2528 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2529 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2530 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear system,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2531 \textcolor{comment}{           ! which  results  in  significant  performance   penalty   when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2532 \textcolor{comment}{           ! compared with "{}fast"{}  version  which  just  calls  triangular}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2533 \textcolor{comment}{           ! solver. Amount of  overhead  introduced  depends  on  M  (the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2534 \textcolor{comment}{           ! larger -\/ the more efficient).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2535 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2536 \textcolor{comment}{           ! This performance penalty is insignificant  when compared with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2537 \textcolor{comment}{           ! cost of large Cholesky decomposition.  However,  if  you call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2538 \textcolor{comment}{           ! this  function  many  times  for  the same  left  side,  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2539 \textcolor{comment}{           ! overhead BECOMES significant. It  also   becomes  significant}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2540 \textcolor{comment}{           ! for small-\/scale problems (N<50).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2541 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2542 \textcolor{comment}{           ! In such cases we strongly recommend you to use faster solver,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2543 \textcolor{comment}{           ! HPDMatrixCholeskySolveMFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2544 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2545 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2546 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2547 \textcolor{comment}{    CHA     -\/   array[N,N], Cholesky decomposition,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2548 \textcolor{comment}{                HPDMatrixCholesky result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2549 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of CHA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2550 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   what half of CHA is provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2551 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[N,M], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2552 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   right part size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2553 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2554 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2555 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2556 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    A is singular, or VERY close to singular.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2557 \textcolor{comment}{                        X is filled by zeros in such cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2558 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2559 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task was solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2560 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   additional report, following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2561 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.r1    condition number in 1-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2562 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.rinf  condition number in inf-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2563 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2564 \textcolor{comment}{                * for info>0 contains solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2565 \textcolor{comment}{                * for info=-\/3 filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2566 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2567 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2568 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 27.01.2010 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2569 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2570 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} hpdmatrixcholeskysolvem(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1complex__2d__array}{complex\_2d\_array}} \&cha, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} isupper, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1complex__2d__array}{complex\_2d\_array}} \&b, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t m, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1densesolverreport}{densesolverreport}} \&rep, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1complex__2d__array}{complex\_2d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}

\DoxyCodeLine{2608 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver for A*x=b with N*N Hermitian positive definite matrix A given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2609 \textcolor{comment}{by its Cholesky decomposition, and N*1 complex vectors x and  b.  This  is}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2612 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2613 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2614 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2615 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2616 \textcolor{comment}{* condition number estimation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2617 \textcolor{comment}{* matrix is represented by its upper or lower triangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2618 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2619 \textcolor{comment}{No iterative refinement is provided because such partial representation of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2620 \textcolor{comment}{matrix does not allow efficient calculation of extra-\/precise  matrix-\/vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2621 \textcolor{comment}{products for large matrices. Use RMatrixSolve or RMatrixMixedSolve  if  you}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2624 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: ! this function is NOT the most efficient linear solver provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2625 \textcolor{comment}{           ! by ALGLIB. It estimates condition  number  of  linear system,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2626 \textcolor{comment}{           ! which results in 10-\/15x  performance  penalty  when  compared}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2627 \textcolor{comment}{           ! with "{}fast"{} version which just calls triangular solver.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2632 \textcolor{comment}{           ! BECOMES significant. It  also  becomes significant for small-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2633 \textcolor{comment}{           ! scale problems (N<50).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2634 \textcolor{comment}{           !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2635 \textcolor{comment}{           ! In such cases we strongly recommend you to use faster solver,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2636 \textcolor{comment}{           ! HPDMatrixCholeskySolveFast() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2637 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2638 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2639 \textcolor{comment}{    CHA     -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], Cholesky decomposition,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2640 \textcolor{comment}{                SPDMatrixCholesky result}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2642 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   what half of CHA is provided}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2647 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    A is is exactly singular or ill conditioned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2648 \textcolor{comment}{                        X is filled by zeros in such cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2649 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2653 \textcolor{comment}{                * rep.rinf  condition number in inf-\/norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2654 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2655 \textcolor{comment}{                * for info>0  -\/ solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2656 \textcolor{comment}{                * for info=-\/3 -\/ filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2657 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2660 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2661 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} hpdmatrixcholeskysolve(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1complex__2d__array}{complex\_2d\_array}} \&cha, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} isupper, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1complex__1d__array}{complex\_1d\_array}} \&b, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1densesolverreport}{densesolverreport}} \&rep, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1complex__1d__array}{complex\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2662 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2663 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2664 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2665 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver for A*x=b with N*N Hermitian positive definite matrix A given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2666 \textcolor{comment}{by its Cholesky decomposition, and N*1 complex vectors x and  b.  This  is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2667 \textcolor{comment}{"{}fast-\/but-\/lightweight"{} version of the solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2668 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2669 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2670 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^2) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2671 \textcolor{comment}{* matrix is represented by its upper or lower triangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2672 \textcolor{comment}{* no additional time-\/consuming features}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2673 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2674 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2675 \textcolor{comment}{    CHA     -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..N-\/1], Cholesky decomposition,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2676 \textcolor{comment}{                SPDMatrixCholesky result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2677 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2678 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   what half of CHA is provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2679 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2680 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2681 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2682 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2683 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    A is is exactly singular or ill conditioned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2684 \textcolor{comment}{                        B is filled by zeros in such cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2685 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    N<=0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2686 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2687 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[N]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2688 \textcolor{comment}{                * for info>0  -\/ overwritten by solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2689 \textcolor{comment}{                * for info=-\/3 -\/ filled by zeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2690 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2691 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2692 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 18.03.2015 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2693 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2694 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} hpdmatrixcholeskysolvefast(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1complex__2d__array}{complex\_2d\_array}} \&cha, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} isupper, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1complex__1d__array}{complex\_1d\_array}} \&b, ae\_int\_t \&info, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2695 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2696 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2697 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2698 \textcolor{comment}{Dense solver.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2699 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2700 \textcolor{comment}{This subroutine finds solution of the linear system A*X=B with non-\/square,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2701 \textcolor{comment}{possibly degenerate A.  System  is  solved in the least squares sense, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2702 \textcolor{comment}{general least squares solution  X = X0 + CX*y  which  minimizes |A*X-\/B| is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2703 \textcolor{comment}{returned. If A is non-\/degenerate, solution in the usual sense is returned.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2704 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2705 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm features:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2706 \textcolor{comment}{* automatic detection (and correct handling!) of degenerate cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2707 \textcolor{comment}{* iterative refinement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2708 \textcolor{comment}{* O(N\string^3) complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2709 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2710 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2711 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   array[0..NRows-\/1,0..NCols-\/1], system matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2712 \textcolor{comment}{    NRows   -\/   vertical size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2713 \textcolor{comment}{    NCols   -\/   horizontal size of A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2714 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   array[0..NCols-\/1], right part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2715 \textcolor{comment}{    Threshold-\/  a number in [0,1]. Singular values  beyond  Threshold  are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2716 \textcolor{comment}{                considered  zero.  Set  it to 0.0, if you don't understand}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2717 \textcolor{comment}{                what it means, so the solver will choose good value on its}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2718 \textcolor{comment}{                own.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2719 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2720 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2721 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   return code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2722 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/4    SVD subroutine failed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2723 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    if NRows<=0 or NCols<=0 or Threshold<0 was passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2724 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    if task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2725 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   solver report, see below for more info}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2726 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..M-\/1], it contains:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2727 \textcolor{comment}{                * solution of A*X=B (even for singular A)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2728 \textcolor{comment}{                * zeros, if SVD subroutine failed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2729 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2730 \textcolor{comment}{SOLVER REPORT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2731 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2732 \textcolor{comment}{Subroutine sets following fields of the Rep structure:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2733 \textcolor{comment}{* R2        reciprocal of condition number: 1/cond(A), 2-\/norm.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2734 \textcolor{comment}{* N         = NCols}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2735 \textcolor{comment}{* K         dim(Null(A))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2736 \textcolor{comment}{* CX        array[0..N-\/1,0..K-\/1], kernel of A.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2737 \textcolor{comment}{            Columns of CX store such vectors that A*CX[i]=0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2738 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2739 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2740 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2741 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Free Edition of ALGLIB supports following important features for  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2742 \textcolor{comment}{  ! function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2743 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C++ version: x64 SIMD support using C++ intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2744 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C\#  version: x64 SIMD support using NET5/NetCore hardware intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2745 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2746 \textcolor{comment}{  ! We  recommend  you  to  read  'Compiling ALGLIB' section of the ALGLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2747 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Reference Manual in order  to  find  out  how to activate SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2748 \textcolor{comment}{  ! in ALGLIB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2749 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2750 \textcolor{comment}{  ! COMMERCIAL EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2751 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2752 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Commercial Edition of ALGLIB includes following important improvements}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2753 \textcolor{comment}{  ! of this function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2754 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * high-\/performance native backend with same C\# interface (C\# version)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2906 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} sparselusolve(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1sparsematrix}{sparsematrix}} \&a, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1integer__1d__array}{integer\_1d\_array}} \&p, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1integer__1d__array}{integer\_1d\_array}} \&q, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&b, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1sparsesolverreport}{sparsesolverreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2907 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2908 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2909 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(AE\_COMPILE\_ITERATIVESPARSE) || !defined(AE\_PARTIAL\_BUILD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2910 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2911 \textcolor{comment}{Solving sparse symmetric linear system A*x=b using GMRES(k) method. Sparse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2912 \textcolor{comment}{symmetric A is given by its lower or upper triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2913 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2914 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: use SparseSolveGMRES() to solve system with nonsymmetric A.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2915 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2916 \textcolor{comment}{This function provides convenience API for an 'expert' interface  provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2917 \textcolor{comment}{by SparseSolverState class. Use SparseSolver  API  if  you  need  advanced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2918 \textcolor{comment}{functions like providing initial point, using out-\/of-\/core API and so on.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2919 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2920 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2921 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   sparse symmetric NxN matrix in any sparse storage  format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2922 \textcolor{comment}{                Using CRS format is recommended because it avoids internal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2923 \textcolor{comment}{                conversion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2924 \textcolor{comment}{                An exception will be generated if  A  is  not  NxN  matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2925 \textcolor{comment}{                (where  N  is  a  size   specified  during  solver  object}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2926 \textcolor{comment}{                creation).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2927 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   whether upper or lower triangle of A is used:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2928 \textcolor{comment}{                * IsUpper=True  => only upper triangle is used and lower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2929 \textcolor{comment}{                                   triangle is not referenced at all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2930 \textcolor{comment}{                * IsUpper=False => only lower triangle is used and upper}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2931 \textcolor{comment}{                                   triangle is not referenced at all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2932 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   right part, array[N]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2933 \textcolor{comment}{    K       -\/   k parameter for  GMRES(k), k>=0.  Zero  value  means  that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2934 \textcolor{comment}{                algorithm will choose it automatically.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2935 \textcolor{comment}{    EpsF    -\/   stopping condition, EpsF>=0. The algorithm will stop  when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2936 \textcolor{comment}{                residual will decrease below EpsF*|B|. Having EpsF=0 means}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2937 \textcolor{comment}{                that this stopping condition is ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2938 \textcolor{comment}{    MaxIts  -\/   stopping condition, MaxIts>=0.  The  algorithm  will  stop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2939 \textcolor{comment}{                after performing MaxIts iterations. Zero  value  means  no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2940 \textcolor{comment}{                limit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2941 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2942 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: having both EpsF=0 and MaxIts=0 means that stopping criteria will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2943 \textcolor{comment}{      chosen automatically.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2944 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2945 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2946 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], the solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2947 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   solution report:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2948 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.TerminationType completion code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2949 \textcolor{comment}{                    * -\/5    CG method was used for a matrix which  is  not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2950 \textcolor{comment}{                            positive definite}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2951 \textcolor{comment}{                    * -\/4    overflow/underflow during solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2952 \textcolor{comment}{                            (ill conditioned problem)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2953 \textcolor{comment}{                    *  1    ||residual||<=EpsF*||b||}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2954 \textcolor{comment}{                    *  5    MaxIts steps was taken}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2955 \textcolor{comment}{                    *  7    rounding errors prevent further progress,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2956 \textcolor{comment}{                            best point found is returned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2957 \textcolor{comment}{                    *  8    the  algorithm  was  terminated   early  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2958 \textcolor{comment}{                            SparseSolverRequestTermination() being called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2959 \textcolor{comment}{                            from other thread.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2960 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.IterationsCount contains iterations count}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2961 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.NMV contains number of matrix-\/vector calculations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2962 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.R2 contains squared residual}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2963 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2964 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2965 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 25.09.2021 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2966 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3020 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3021 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3022 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3023 \textcolor{comment}{This function initializes sparse linear iterative solver object.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3024 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3025 \textcolor{comment}{This solver can be used  to  solve  nonsymmetric  and  symmetric  positive}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3026 \textcolor{comment}{definite NxN (square) linear systems.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3027 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3028 \textcolor{comment}{The solver provides  'expert'  API  which  allows  advanced  control  over}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3029 \textcolor{comment}{algorithms being used, including ability to get progress report, terminate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3030 \textcolor{comment}{long-\/running solver from other thread, out-\/of-\/core solution and so on.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3031 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3032 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: there are also convenience  functions  that  allows  quick  one-\/line}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3033 \textcolor{comment}{      access to the solvers:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3034 \textcolor{comment}{      * SparseSolveCG() to solve SPD linear systems}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3035 \textcolor{comment}{      * SparseSolveGMRES() to solve unsymmetric linear systems.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3036 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3037 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: if you want to solve MxN (rectangular) linear problem  you  may  use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3038 \textcolor{comment}{      LinLSQR solver provided by ALGLIB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3039 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3040 \textcolor{comment}{USAGE (A is given by the SparseMatrix structure):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3041 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3042 \textcolor{comment}{    1. User initializes algorithm state with SparseSolverCreate() call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3043 \textcolor{comment}{    2. User  selects   algorithm  with one of the SparseSolverSetAlgo???()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3044 \textcolor{comment}{       functions. By default, GMRES(k) is used with automatically chosen k}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3045 \textcolor{comment}{    3. Optionally, user tunes solver parameters, sets starting point, etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3046 \textcolor{comment}{    4. Depending on whether system is symmetric or not, user calls:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3047 \textcolor{comment}{       * SparseSolverSolveSymmetric() for a  symmetric system given by its}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3048 \textcolor{comment}{         lower or upper triangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3049 \textcolor{comment}{       * SparseSolverSolve() for a nonsymmetric system or a symmetric  one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3050 \textcolor{comment}{         given by the full matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3051 \textcolor{comment}{    5. User calls SparseSolverResults() to get the solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3052 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3053 \textcolor{comment}{    It is possible to call SparseSolverSolve???() again to  solve  another}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3054 \textcolor{comment}{    task with same dimensionality but different matrix and/or  right  part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3055 \textcolor{comment}{    without reinitializing SparseSolverState structure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3056 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3057 \textcolor{comment}{USAGE (out-\/of-\/core mode):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3058 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3059 \textcolor{comment}{    1. User initializes algorithm state with SparseSolverCreate() call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3060 \textcolor{comment}{    2. User  selects   algorithm  with one of the SparseSolverSetAlgo???()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3061 \textcolor{comment}{       functions. By default, GMRES(k) is used with automatically chosen k}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3062 \textcolor{comment}{    3. Optionally, user tunes solver parameters, sets starting point, etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3063 \textcolor{comment}{    4. After that user should work with out-\/of-\/core interface  in  a  loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3064 \textcolor{comment}{       like one given below:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3065 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3066 \textcolor{comment}{        > alglib.sparsesolveroocstart(state)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3067 \textcolor{comment}{        > while alglib.sparsesolverooccontinue(state) do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3068 \textcolor{comment}{        >     alglib.sparsesolveroocgetrequestinfo(state, out RequestType)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3069 \textcolor{comment}{        >     alglib.sparsesolveroocgetrequestdata(state, out X)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3070 \textcolor{comment}{        >     if RequestType=0 then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3071 \textcolor{comment}{        >         [calculate  Y=A*X, with X=R\string^N]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3072 \textcolor{comment}{        >     alglib.sparsesolveroocsendresult(state, in Y)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3073 \textcolor{comment}{        > alglib.sparsesolveroocstop(state, out X, out Report)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3074 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3075 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3076 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   problem dimensionality (fixed at start-\/up)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3077 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3078 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3079 \textcolor{comment}{    State   -\/   structure which stores algorithm state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3080 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3081 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3082 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 24.09.2021 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3083 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3084 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} sparsesolvercreate(\textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1sparsesolverstate}{sparsesolverstate}} \&state, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3087 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3089 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3090 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: if you do not need advanced functionality of the  SparseSolver  API,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3097 \textcolor{comment}{                * recommended values are in 10..100 range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3098 \textcolor{comment}{                * larger values up to N are possible but have little sense}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3099 \textcolor{comment}{                  -\/ the algorithm will be slower than any dense solver.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3102 \textcolor{comment}{                  value is 50 in the current version, but  it  may  change}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3103 \textcolor{comment}{                  in future ALGLIB releases.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3149 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3150 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3151 \textcolor{comment}{Procedure for  the  solution of A*x=b with sparse symmetric A given by its}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3152 \textcolor{comment}{lower or upper triangle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3153 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3154 \textcolor{comment}{This function will work with any solver algorithm  being   used,  SPD  one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3155 \textcolor{comment}{(like CG) or not (like GMRES). Using unsymmetric solvers (like  GMRES)  on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3156 \textcolor{comment}{SPD problems is suboptimal, but still possible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3157 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3158 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: the  solver  behavior is ill-\/defined  for  a  situation  when a  SPD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3159 \textcolor{comment}{      solver is used on indefinite matrix. It  may solve the problem up to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3160 \textcolor{comment}{      desired precision (sometimes, rarely)  or  return  with  error  code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3161 \textcolor{comment}{      signalling violation of underlying assumptions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3162 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3163 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3164 \textcolor{comment}{    State   -\/   algorithm state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3165 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   sparse symmetric NxN matrix in any sparse storage  format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3166 \textcolor{comment}{                Using CRS format is recommended because it avoids internal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3167 \textcolor{comment}{                conversion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3168 \textcolor{comment}{                An exception will be generated if  A  is  not  NxN  matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3169 \textcolor{comment}{                (where  N  is  a  size   specified  during  solver  object}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3170 \textcolor{comment}{                creation).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3171 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   whether upper or lower triangle of A is used:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3172 \textcolor{comment}{                * IsUpper=True  => only upper triangle is used and lower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3173 \textcolor{comment}{                                   triangle is not referenced at all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3174 \textcolor{comment}{                * IsUpper=False => only lower triangle is used and upper}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3175 \textcolor{comment}{                                   triangle is not referenced at all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3176 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   right part, array[N]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3177 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3178 \textcolor{comment}{RESULT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3179 \textcolor{comment}{    This function returns no result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3180 \textcolor{comment}{    You can get the solution by calling SparseSolverResults()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3181 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3182 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3183 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 25.09.2021 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3184 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3188 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3189 \textcolor{comment}{Procedure for the solution of A*x=b with sparse nonsymmetric A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3190 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3191 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: this function will work with any solver algorithm  being  used,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3192 \textcolor{comment}{           symmetric solver like CG,  or  not.  However,  using  symmetric}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3193 \textcolor{comment}{           solvers on nonsymmetric problems is  dangerous.  It  may  solve}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3194 \textcolor{comment}{           the problem up  to  desired  precision  (sometimes,  rarely) or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3195 \textcolor{comment}{           terminate with error code signalling  violation  of  underlying}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3196 \textcolor{comment}{           assumptions.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3202 \textcolor{comment}{                conversion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3203 \textcolor{comment}{                An exception will be generated if  A  is  not  NxN  matrix}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3205 \textcolor{comment}{                creation).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3227 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3228 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3229 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   solution report:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3230 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.TerminationType completion code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3231 \textcolor{comment}{                    * -\/5    CG method was used for a matrix which  is  not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3232 \textcolor{comment}{                            positive definite}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3233 \textcolor{comment}{                    * -\/4    overflow/underflow during solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3234 \textcolor{comment}{                            (ill conditioned problem)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3235 \textcolor{comment}{                    *  1    ||residual||<=EpsF*||b||}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3236 \textcolor{comment}{                    *  5    MaxIts steps was taken}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3237 \textcolor{comment}{                    *  7    rounding errors prevent further progress,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3238 \textcolor{comment}{                            best point found is returned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3239 \textcolor{comment}{                    *  8    the  algorithm  was  terminated   early  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3240 \textcolor{comment}{                            SparseSolverRequestTermination() being called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3241 \textcolor{comment}{                            from other thread.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3242 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.IterationsCount contains iterations count}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3243 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.NMV contains number of matrix-\/vector calculations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3244 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.R2 contains squared residual}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3245 \textcolor{comment}{s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3246 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3252 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3253 \textcolor{comment}{This function turns on/off reporting during out-\/of-\/core processing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3254 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3255 \textcolor{comment}{When the solver works in the out-\/of-\/core mode, it  can  be  configured  to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3256 \textcolor{comment}{report its progress by returning current location. These location  reports}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3257 \textcolor{comment}{are implemented as a special kind of the out-\/of-\/core request:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3258 \textcolor{comment}{* SparseSolverOOCGetRequestInfo() returns -\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3259 \textcolor{comment}{* SparseSolverOOCGetRequestData() returns current location}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3260 \textcolor{comment}{* SparseSolverOOCGetRequestData1() returns squared norm of the residual}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3261 \textcolor{comment}{* SparseSolverOOCSendResult() shall NOT be called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3262 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3263 \textcolor{comment}{This function has no effect when SparseSolverSolve() is used because  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3264 \textcolor{comment}{function has no method of reporting its progress.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3265 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3266 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: when used with GMRES(k), this function reports progress  every  k-\/th}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3267 \textcolor{comment}{      iteration.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3268 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3269 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3270 \textcolor{comment}{    State   -\/   structure which stores algorithm state}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3273 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3442 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3443 \textcolor{comment}{This  function  finalizes out-\/of-\/core mode of the linear solver. It should}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3444 \textcolor{comment}{be used in conjunction with other out-\/of-\/core-\/related  functions  of  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3445 \textcolor{comment}{subspackage in a loop like one given below:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3446 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3447 \textcolor{comment}{> alglib.sparsesolveroocstart(state)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3448 \textcolor{comment}{> while alglib.sparsesolverooccontinue(state) do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3449 \textcolor{comment}{>     alglib.sparsesolveroocgetrequestinfo(state, out RequestType)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3450 \textcolor{comment}{>     alglib.sparsesolveroocgetrequestdata(state, out X)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3451 \textcolor{comment}{>     if RequestType=0 then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3452 \textcolor{comment}{>         [calculate  Y=A*X, with X=R\string^N]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3453 \textcolor{comment}{>     alglib.sparsesolveroocsendresult(state, in Y)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3454 \textcolor{comment}{> alglib.sparsesolveroocstop(state, out X, out Report)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3455 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3456 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3457 \textcolor{comment}{    State       -\/   solver state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3458 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3459 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3460 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], the solution.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3461 \textcolor{comment}{                Zero-\/filled on the failure (Rep.TerminationType<0).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3462 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   report with additional info:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3463 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.TerminationType completion code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3464 \textcolor{comment}{                    * -\/5    CG method was used for a matrix which  is  not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3465 \textcolor{comment}{                            positive definite}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3466 \textcolor{comment}{                    * -\/4    overflow/underflow during solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3467 \textcolor{comment}{                            (ill conditioned problem)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3468 \textcolor{comment}{                    *  1    ||residual||<=EpsF*||b||}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3469 \textcolor{comment}{                    *  5    MaxIts steps was taken}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3470 \textcolor{comment}{                    *  7    rounding errors prevent further progress,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3471 \textcolor{comment}{                            best point found is returned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3472 \textcolor{comment}{                    *  8    the  algorithm  was  terminated   early  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3473 \textcolor{comment}{                            SparseSolverRequestTermination() being called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3474 \textcolor{comment}{                            from other thread.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3475 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.IterationsCount contains iterations count}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3476 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.NMV contains number of matrix-\/vector calculations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3477 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.R2 contains squared residual}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3478 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3479 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3480 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 24.09.2021 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3481 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3485 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3486 \textcolor{comment}{This subroutine submits request for termination of the running solver.  It}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3487 \textcolor{comment}{can be called from some other thread which wants the   solver to terminate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3488 \textcolor{comment}{or when processing an out-\/of-\/core request.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3489 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3490 \textcolor{comment}{As result, solver  stops  at  point  which  was  "{}current  accepted"{}  when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3491 \textcolor{comment}{the termination request was submitted and returns error code 8 (successful}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3492 \textcolor{comment}{termination).  Such   termination   is  a smooth  process  which  properly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3493 \textcolor{comment}{deallocates all temporaries.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3494 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3495 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3496 \textcolor{comment}{    State   -\/   solver structure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3497 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3498 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: calling this function on solver which is NOT running  will  have  no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3499 \textcolor{comment}{      effect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3500 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: multiple calls to this function are possible. First call is counted,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3502 \textcolor{comment}{      subsequent calls are silently ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3503 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: solver clears termination flag on its start, it means that  if  some}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3505 \textcolor{comment}{      other thread will request termination too soon, its request will went}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3506 \textcolor{comment}{      unnoticed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3507 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3508 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3509 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 01.10.2021 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3510 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3517 \textcolor{comment}{symmetric positive definite problems. If you want  to  solve  nonsymmetric}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3518 \textcolor{comment}{(or non-\/positive definite) problem you may use LinLSQR solver provided  by}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3520 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3522 \textcolor{comment}{1. User initializes algorithm state with LinCGCreate() call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3523 \textcolor{comment}{2. User tunes solver parameters with  LinCGSetCond() and other functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3524 \textcolor{comment}{3. Optionally, user sets starting point with LinCGSetStartingPoint()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3525 \textcolor{comment}{4. User  calls LinCGSolveSparse() function which takes algorithm state and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3526 \textcolor{comment}{   SparseMatrix object.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3527 \textcolor{comment}{5. User calls LinCGResults() to get solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3528 \textcolor{comment}{6. Optionally, user may call LinCGSolveSparse()  again  to  solve  another}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3529 \textcolor{comment}{   problem  with different matrix and/or right part without reinitializing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3530 \textcolor{comment}{   LinCGState structure.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3611 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3612 \textcolor{comment}{Procedure for solution of A*x=b with sparse A.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3613 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3614 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3615 \textcolor{comment}{    State   -\/   algorithm state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3616 \textcolor{comment}{    A       -\/   sparse matrix in the CRS format (you MUST contvert  it  to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3617 \textcolor{comment}{                CRS format by calling SparseConvertToCRS() function).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3618 \textcolor{comment}{    IsUpper -\/   whether upper or lower triangle of A is used:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3619 \textcolor{comment}{                * IsUpper=True  => only upper triangle is used and lower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3620 \textcolor{comment}{                                   triangle is not referenced at all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3621 \textcolor{comment}{                * IsUpper=False => only lower triangle is used and upper}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3622 \textcolor{comment}{                                   triangle is not referenced at all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3623 \textcolor{comment}{    B       -\/   right part, array[N]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3624 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3625 \textcolor{comment}{RESULT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3626 \textcolor{comment}{    This function returns no result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3627 \textcolor{comment}{    You can get solution by calling LinCGResults()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3628 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3629 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: this function uses lightweight preconditioning -\/  multiplication  by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3630 \textcolor{comment}{      inverse of diag(A). If you want, you can turn preconditioning off by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3631 \textcolor{comment}{      calling LinCGSetPrecUnit(). However, preconditioning cost is low and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3632 \textcolor{comment}{      preconditioner  is  very  important  for  solution  of  badly scaled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3633 \textcolor{comment}{      problems.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3634 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3635 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3680 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3681 \textcolor{comment}{This function sets frequency of residual recalculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3682 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3683 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm updates residual r\_k using iterative formula,  but  recalculates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3684 \textcolor{comment}{it from scratch after each 10 iterations. It is done to avoid accumulation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3685 \textcolor{comment}{of numerical errors and to stop algorithm when r\_k starts to grow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3686 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3687 \textcolor{comment}{Such low update frequence (1/10) gives very  little  overhead,  but  makes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3688 \textcolor{comment}{algorithm a bit more robust against numerical errors. However, you may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3689 \textcolor{comment}{change it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3690 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3691 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3692 \textcolor{comment}{    Freq    -\/   desired update frequency, Freq>=0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3693 \textcolor{comment}{                Zero value means that no updates will be done.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3694 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3695 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3696 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 14.11.2011 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3697 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3698 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} lincgsetrupdatefreq(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1lincgstate}{lincgstate}} \&state, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t freq, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3720 \textcolor{comment}{non-\/symmetric (and, possibly, non-\/square) problems. Least squares solution}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3918 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3919 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3920 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3921 \textcolor{comment}{This subroutine submits request for termination of the running solver.  It}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3922 \textcolor{comment}{can be called from some other thread which wants LSQR solver to  terminate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3923 \textcolor{comment}{(obviously, the  thread  running  LSQR  solver can not request termination}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3924 \textcolor{comment}{because it is already busy working on LSQR).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3925 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3926 \textcolor{comment}{As result, solver  stops  at  point  which  was  "{}current  accepted"{}  when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3927 \textcolor{comment}{termination  request  was  submitted  and returns error code 8 (successful}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3928 \textcolor{comment}{termination).  Such   termination   is  a smooth  process  which  properly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3929 \textcolor{comment}{deallocates all temporaries.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3930 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3931 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3932 \textcolor{comment}{    State   -\/   solver structure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3933 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3934 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: calling this function on solver which is NOT running  will  have  no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3935 \textcolor{comment}{      effect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3936 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3937 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: multiple calls to this function are possible. First call is counted,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3938 \textcolor{comment}{      subsequent calls are silently ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3939 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3940 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: solver clears termination flag on its start, it means that  if  some}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3941 \textcolor{comment}{      other thread will request termination too soon, its request will went}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3942 \textcolor{comment}{      unnoticed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3943 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3944 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3945 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 08.10.2014 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3946 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3947 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} linlsqrrequesttermination(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1linlsqrstate}{linlsqrstate}} \&state, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3948 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3949 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3950 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(AE\_COMPILE\_NLEQ) || !defined(AE\_PARTIAL\_BUILD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3951 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3952 \textcolor{comment}{                LEVENBERG-\/MARQUARDT-\/LIKE NONLINEAR SOLVER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3953 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3954 \textcolor{comment}{DESCRIPTION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3955 \textcolor{comment}{This algorithm solves system of nonlinear equations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3956 \textcolor{comment}{    F[0](x[0], ..., x[n-\/1])   = 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3957 \textcolor{comment}{    F[1](x[0], ..., x[n-\/1])   = 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3958 \textcolor{comment}{    ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3959 \textcolor{comment}{    F[M-\/1](x[0], ..., x[n-\/1]) = 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3960 \textcolor{comment}{with M/N do not necessarily coincide.  Algorithm  converges  quadratically}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3961 \textcolor{comment}{under following conditions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3962 \textcolor{comment}{    * the solution set XS is nonempty}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3963 \textcolor{comment}{    * for some xs in XS there exist such neighbourhood N(xs) that:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3964 \textcolor{comment}{      * vector function F(x) and its Jacobian J(x) are continuously}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3965 \textcolor{comment}{        differentiable on N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3966 \textcolor{comment}{      * ||F(x)|| provides local error bound on N, i.e. there  exists  such}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3967 \textcolor{comment}{        c1, that ||F(x)||>c1*distance(x,XS)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3968 \textcolor{comment}{Note that these conditions are much more weaker than usual non-\/singularity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3969 \textcolor{comment}{conditions. For example, algorithm will converge for any  affine  function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3970 \textcolor{comment}{F (whether its Jacobian singular or not).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3971 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3972 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3973 \textcolor{comment}{REQUIREMENTS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3974 \textcolor{comment}{Algorithm will request following information during its operation:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3975 \textcolor{comment}{* function vector F[] and Jacobian matrix at given point X}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3976 \textcolor{comment}{* value of merit function f(x)=F[0]\string^2(x)+...+F[M-\/1]\string^2(x) at given point X}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3977 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3978 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3979 \textcolor{comment}{USAGE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3980 \textcolor{comment}{1. User initializes algorithm state with NLEQCreateLM() call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3981 \textcolor{comment}{2. User tunes solver parameters with  NLEQSetCond(),  NLEQSetStpMax()  and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3982 \textcolor{comment}{   other functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3983 \textcolor{comment}{3. User  calls  NLEQSolve()  function  which  takes  algorithm  state  and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3984 \textcolor{comment}{   pointers (delegates, etc.) to callback functions which calculate  merit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3985 \textcolor{comment}{   function value and Jacobian.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3986 \textcolor{comment}{4. User calls NLEQResults() to get solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3987 \textcolor{comment}{5. Optionally, user may call NLEQRestartFrom() to  solve  another  problem}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3988 \textcolor{comment}{   with same parameters (N/M) but another starting  point  and/or  another}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3989 \textcolor{comment}{   function vector. NLEQRestartFrom() allows to reuse already  initialized}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3990 \textcolor{comment}{   structure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3991 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3992 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3993 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3994 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   space dimension, N>1:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3995 \textcolor{comment}{                * if provided, only leading N elements of X are used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3996 \textcolor{comment}{                * if not provided, determined automatically from size of X}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3997 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   system size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3998 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   starting point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3999 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4000 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4001 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4002 \textcolor{comment}{    State   -\/   structure which stores algorithm state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4003 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4004 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4005 \textcolor{comment}{NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4006 \textcolor{comment}{1. you may tune stopping conditions with NLEQSetCond() function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4007 \textcolor{comment}{2. if target function contains exp() or other fast growing functions,  and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4008 \textcolor{comment}{   optimization algorithm makes too large steps which leads  to  overflow,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4009 \textcolor{comment}{   use NLEQSetStpMax() function to bound algorithm's steps.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4010 \textcolor{comment}{3. this  algorithm  is  a  slightly  modified implementation of the method}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4011 \textcolor{comment}{   described  in  'Levenberg-\/Marquardt  method  for constrained  nonlinear}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4012 \textcolor{comment}{   equations with strong local convergence properties' by Christian Kanzow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4013 \textcolor{comment}{   Nobuo Yamashita and Masao Fukushima and further  developed  in  'On the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4014 \textcolor{comment}{   convergence of a New Levenberg-\/Marquardt Method'  by  Jin-\/yan  Fan  and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4015 \textcolor{comment}{   Ya-\/Xiang Yuan.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4016 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4017 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4018 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4019 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 20.08.2009 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4020 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4021 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} nleqcreatelm(\textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t m, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1nleqstate}{nleqstate}} \&state, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
